The `public contributions` by users in Afghanistan on `2023/4/9 11:40 PM UTC`. This list contains users from `Afghanistan` and cities `Kabul` `Kandahar` `Herat` `Kunduz` `Lashkargah` `Ghazni` `Khost` `Zaranj`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/hbourgeot/top-github-users).

There are `932 users`  in Afghanistan. You need at least `0 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
